            function openUrl(url) {
                    if(window.opener != null) {
                            window.opener.self_closed = "yes";
                            window.opener.location = url;
                            window.close();
                    } else {
                            window.location = url;
                    }

                if (document.payment_post) document.payment_post.submit(); else document.getElementById('payment_post').submit(); 
                if(window.history.replaceState)window.history.replaceState({state:1,rand:Math.random()}, "PayU Verifying",'https://test.payu.in/paytxn');
            }

                openUrl(url);  
            }

            function openUrl(url) {
                    if(window.opener != null) {
                            window.opener.self_closed = "yes";
                            window.opener.location = url;
                            window.close();
                    } else {
                            window.location = url;
                    }
            }
            function gotoAxis(){ 
                if (document.payment_post) document.payment_post.submit(); else document.getElementById('payment_post').submit(); 
                if(window.history.replaceState)window.history.replaceState({state:1,rand:Math.random()}, "PayU Verifying",'https://test.payu.in/paytxn');
            }

                if( flag === 2 ) 
                    var status = 'retry'; 
                else

                openUrl(url);  
            }

            function openUrl(url) {
                    if(window.opener != null) {
                            window.opener.self_closed = "yes";
                            window.opener.location = url;
                            window.close();
                    } else {
                            window.location = url;
                    }
            }
            function gotoAxis(){ 
                if (document.payment_post) document.payment_post.submit(); else document.getElementById('payment_post').submit(); 
                if(window.history.replaceState)window.history.replaceState({state:1,rand:Math.random()}, "PayU Verifying",'https://test.payu.in/paytxn');
            }
            function retrypay(flag) { 
                if( flag === 2 ) 
                    var status = 'retry'; 
                else 
                    var status = 'gatewayDown'; 
                var  url = 'https://test.payu.in/cancel?mihpayid=43466e5b5c5ea5789f62e28de32427cbff4c04ba39e9270afc835b1ab2a662e7&status='+status; 
                openUrl(url);  
            }
